*Grade 1 Maths — June Quiz*
_4012 questions (4012 new + 0 revision)_

*Q1.* 🔢 In ascending order, which number comes in the MIDDLE? 25, 1, 19
A) 1
B) 19
C) 25
D) 20
✅ *Answer:* B) 19
💡 Sorted: 1, 19, 25; middle is 19.
━━━━━━━━━━
*Q2.* 🧱 4 tens and 8 ones make which number?
A) 47
B) 50
C) 48
D) 84
✅ *Answer:* C) 48
💡 4 tens + 8 ones = 48.
